English: My forbears, the old men and women folk, were of the Mexican People Clan. With great hardship they came back from the place called Fort Sumner, packing their goods on their backs, and afterward lived here at Lukachukai.
Gold: Shadahastóí ńt’éé’ ’índa dashimá sání ńt’éé’ Naakaii Dine’é danilį́įgo hojoobá’ígo Hwééldi hoolyéédę́ę́’ nináda’iishjidgo kwii Lók’a’jígai hoolyéegi kéédahat’į́į́ ńt’éé’
Translation: Shinaagóó hastiin sání dóó sáanii Naakaii Dine’é nilį́į’. Ayóó hodichééhgo Hwéeldi góne’ náádiikah, bee’eldǫǫ’ bik’ijį’ yigháhgo, ádíí’ k’ad díí Lók’aa’ch’egai déé’ nidaalyaa.

English: Here they began life anew.
Gold: Kodóó shį́į́ haakai nahalin silį́į́’
Translation: ’Éí kwe’é iiná náá hajííní’go diits’ą́’

English: Then from their home at a place called Spring in the Clay they started moving over and across yonder mountain.
Gold: Dleesh Bii’ Tó hoolyéegi dahooghan ńt’ée’go dah ’adiiná jiní nagháí dził báátis gó’ąą
Translation: Ńt’éé’ Bis Tó hoolyé’ígíí bighan góne’ nagháí dził yikah deyááh.

English: While they were making this move they stopped for the night, and it is said that I was born where they halted.
Gold: ’Ákǫ́ǫ́ ’oonéełgo dahwiiłkaahgo ’ákwii shi’dizhchį́ jiní
Translation: Díí ’áhoot’é’ígíí bits’ąą’ na’oolkiłgo da’diists’ą́ą́’, dóó da’diists’ą́ą́’gi shijishchį́į’ jiní.

English: Let’s see, I believe it was in the month of October
Gold: Ghąąjį’ wolyéego ńdízídígíí daashin t’áá ’éí biyi’ jiní
Translation: Háálá’, Gháájí’di wooshdlą́ą.

English: I was born on a night when a heavy snow had begun to fall.
Gold: Tł’ée’go hááhgóóshį́į́ deezhchxíilgo ts’ídá ’ákóne’ shi’dizhchį́ jiní
Translation: Chahałhééhdi yéego yas deeslį́ígíí shi’dizhchį́.

English: My grandfather, a man by the name of White Mexican Clansman, and another man called The Son of Former Sweathouse, were the only men. They and several womenfolk worked hard on me.
Gold: Shichei ńt’éé’ Naakai Dine’é Łigaii wolyéé ńt’éé’ dóó ła’ dó’ Diné Táchéhéni’ Biye’ wolyéé ńt’éé’ ’éí shį́į́ t’éiyá diné nilį́įgo dóó sáanii dó’ díkwíí shį́į́ kwii shaa naanish bííghą́ą́’
Translation: Shichei, Hastiin Naakaii Dine’é Łigaii wolyéé ńt’éé’, dóó ła’ Hastiin ’áádę́ę́’ Hooghan Táchééh Biyázhí wolyéé ńt’éé’, ’éí t’áá íiyisí hastiinii. ’Éí dóó haa shį́į́ ’asdzání łizhgo shił na’anish.

English: My grandfather had a fine wether goat that he was quite proud of. He killed it there, and the people feasted with great joy.
Gold: Shichei tł’ízí cho’ádinii ’ayói da ’át’é halį́į́’ ńt’ée’go ’éí ’ákwii jiisxį́įgo hááhgóóshį́į́ diné bił dahózhǫ́ǫgo da’oolghal jiní
Translation: Shicheii tł’ízí yilbááh nizhóní bił hólǫ́; éí baa hodíílzíní. ’Ákwii tł’ízí yilbááh yílts’ą́’; áádóó diné ts’ídá nizhónígo ’ajílwo’go adiyį́į́’.

English: Then on the day following the night of my birth we again started to move.
Gold: Tł’éédą́ą́’ shi’dizhchį́įgo t’áá ’áko dah náá’dii’ná jiní
Translation: ’Aadóó tł’éédą́ą́’ shijishchį́įgo ’áajį’go t’áá ni’ dah náádiikai

English: In those days people went about only on horseback
Gold: ’Íídą́ą́’ łį́į́’ t’éiyá bee nda’aldeehgo
Translation: Ádíí’go diné t’áá łį́į́’ bił náá’nálwod

English: or afoot.
Gold: T’áá ni’ dó’
Translation: T’áá ni’

English: On the day following the night on which she gave birth to me, my mother went on foot as far as the people moved that day.
Gold: Shimá tł’éédą́ą́’ shijishchį́įgo t’áá ni’ jiníyá jiní níwohjį’ haa shį́į́ nízahgi ni’ínéehgo ’áajį’
Translation: Tł’éédą́ą́’ shi’dizhchį́įgo diné danááhígóó shimá deeyá jiní

English: And since it had snowed the night before they had to go through the snow.
Gold: Tł’éédą́ą́’ yidzaazgo yas biyi’ ’íldeé jiní
Translation: Tł’éédą́ą́’ yas hólǫ́go yas bitah deiyáʼ nidi

English: It is remarkable how risky life was in those days.
Gold: Ha’át’íí shį́į́ yówéé ’át’éego diné t’áá bizááká kéédahat’į́į́ ńt’éé’ lá ’íídą́ą́’
Translation: T’áá iiyisígo ’Íídą́ą́’ iiná t’áá ts’ídágo át’į́.

English: Nowadays when a woman gives birth they take special care of her, telling her not to catch cold.
Gold: K’adgo ’éiyá ’ajiłchíihgo hak’az biih wolyeed lágo ha’níigo honídahodéeníih łeh
Translation: Díí shį́į́’go asdzání awéé’ deeshą́ągo, bik’ehgo t’áá ajiłíígíí baa ahoodzááh, doo diists’ą́’ da níigo

English: Back at that time it was different.
Gold: ’Íídą́ą́’ ’éí doo ’ákót’ée da ńt’éé’ lá
Translation: ’Íídą́ą́’ doo t’áá shoodí da.

English: As time went on I somehow grew up. I do not remember much about it.
Gold: ’Áádóó wóshdę́ę́’ haa shį́į́ yit’éego shiyaa hazlį́į́’ ’éí doo ts’ídá hazhó’ó bénáshniih da
Translation: Yiską́ągo t’áá jíík’ehgo shihwiilyá T’áá ’áłts’ó’ doo bénáshniih da

English: I do not remember in detail much of what happened before I was about ten years old.
Gold: Neeznáá daats’í shinááhai dóó ’índa t’áá kóníghání nahalingo ’énáshniihgo hodideeshzhiizh
Translation: ’Áłtsé ts’ídá neeznáá shinááhaigo háádahóót’įįd ’éí doo ts’ídá hazhó’ó bénáshniih da.

English: When morning would come and I would be sleeping nicely, my grandfather would throw me out of bed.
Gold: ’Áyąą ’ahbínígo nizhónígo ’ashhoshę́ę shichei náshidiyiiłhą́ą́h
Translation: ’Áko ’abínígo yá’át’ééhgo ’iideeshhosh nétį́į́, shicheii ts’ídá náshizhdiiłt’e’.

English: Come on! Come on!
Gold: Nahgóó nahgóó
Translation: Haalá! Haalá!

English: Why are you lying down?
Gold: Ha’át’íí biniiyé sínítį́
Translation: Ha’át’íísh baa nidííłkał?

English: Go run a race.
Gold: Nahgóó dághádílyeed
Translation: Nidaazbaa’

English: If you're weak the first harmful thing that comes along will run over you.
Gold: Dinigisgo háadi shį́į́ deeteel t’áá ’áłtsé silį́’ígíí nik’i ch’ídoolwoł
Translation: Doo bidziil níł hólón daago, t’áá ’áłtsé bąąh dah naaznilígíí yááhoot’éego níyoolkááł.

English: If you are strong you will lie hudled in death only after the dirt is torn and furrowed around you (i.e. you will give up only after a struggle)," my grandfather used to tell me.
Gold: Honíyóigo ’éí łeezh naanídaasdláadgo ’áadi ’índa shíníljool dooleeł jiníi łeh ńt’éé’ shichei yę́ę
Translation: Ayóó ’áhoot’éego nílį́ígo, nihá kéyah bikáa’ hadiists’ósgo dóó na’álkidgo ts’ídá éí nít’į́’ dooleeł, shicheii shił yááłti’go jiní.

English: The old folks all used to say that.
Gold: ’Índa hastóí t’áá ’ałtso ’ákódajiníi łeh ńt’éé’
Translation: Sáanii hastóí t’áá’ ałtsoní halne’ ńt’éé’ jiní.

English: They probably said this because they knew of the wars that were going on.
Gold: ’Eíshą’ ’ana dahólóonii hoł béédahózingo ’ádajiníí ńt’éé’
Translation: Na’ídíílwo’ígíí baa danízin biniiyé shį́į́ díí yá.

English: That is the way my grandfather drove me about and spoke to me.
Gold: Shichei yę́ę ’ákót’éego t’áá nashineeyood dóó t’áá shich’į’ yááłti’
Translation: Díígo shichei shí yá yishááł dóó shił yáłti’.

English: He did not speak in anger.
Gold: Doo hashkéego ’áníi da
Translation: Doo k’éshjéé’go ’áníi da

English: He did not speak harshly.
Gold: Doo t’áá na’níle’ee ’áníi da
Translation: Doo íiyisígo ’áníi da

English: He told it to me in a nice way.
Gold: Hazhóó’ógo ’áshiłníí ńt’éé’
Translation: Yá’át’ééhgo shił hojilne’

English: So that is the way I spent my days from that time on.
Gold: Jó ’éí ’áádę́ę́’ ’ákót’éego shíiníłką́
Translation: Áko ’Íídą́ą́’go éí t’áá ’ákót’éego jį́į́d shí éí át’é shį́.

English: After I had reached the age of eighteen I did various kinds of odd jobs.
Gold: Tseebííts’áadah shinááhai sélį́į’go ’áajį’ ’aníísą́ągo jó kodóó shinaanish naat’i’ t’áá bihoniyázhígi
Translation: Tseebííts’áadah shinááhaigo áłk’idá t’áá jíík’ehgo shinaanish adíílníí’.

English: I had an uncle by the name of Forked House. He was a young man, and he adopted me.
Gold: Shidá’í ńt’éé’ T’iisyaa Bikiní wolyéé ńt’éé’ tsíłkę́ę́h nilį́įgo ’éí ’áyaa nikishidiilt’e’
Translation: Shizhé’é yázhí éí Kin Binát’á’í yoolyéé’. Ashkii yázhí nilį́, dóó shí bíyázhí yiníłnii’.

English: He started sending me on chores.
Gold: Nikishidiił’a’
Translation: T’áá ’ádę́ę́’ shí naanish baa ná’jíníłnááh jiní

English: I would take care of his horses for him.
Gold: Łį́į́’ bá naasłóozgo
Translation: Łį́į’ bídádish’ááh.

English: He had a wagon and a team.
Gold: Bitsinaabąąs hólǫ́ǫgo bilį́į́’ na’ałbąąsii hólǫ́ǫgo
Translation: Ha’iilbąąs dóó łį́į’ naaki bił hólǫ́.

English: He would tell me to haul wood with it, or to work with it.
Gold: Díí bee chizh nihíyeeh díí bee nanilnish shiłníigo
Translation: Bee chizh nihoheeh, lágo bee naashnish shił náhálnih.

English: At the time I was about eighteen years old the person who started the present trading post at Blue Clay Point moved there - I used to know just when it was.
Gold: Ts’ídá tseebííts’áadah shinááhaigo Bis Dootł’izh Deez’áhí hoolyéegi k’ad naalyéhé bá hooghan ninínáanii t’áá shił bééhózin ńt’éé’
Translation: Shí t’áá shoodí tseebíí’ ts’áadah nish’áígíígo, Bis Dootł’izh Deez’áhí hoolyéegi díí jį’ hólǫ́ naalyéhé bá hooghan yileehígíí hastiin ’éí kingóó deit’ááh; t’ah ńt’éé’ hazhó’ó bénáshniih.

English: They used to call the Former Old Interpreter (Chee Dodge) Chee (Red) when I first heard of him.
Gold: Hastiin ’Adiits’a’í yę́ęni’ Chíí’ dabijiníí lágo baa ’ákoniizį́į́’
Translation: Shí t’áá áłtsé bił ha’jilné’go, Hastiin ’Adiits’a’í Sání Chii’ (Łichíí’) yiníł’íní.

English: Chee was a good friend of a white man from Ugly House (Manuelito, N.M.) known as Big Lump Setting Up (S.E. Aldrich).
Gold: Kin Hóchxǫ́’í hoolyéédę́ę́’ Bilagáana Dah Shizhóód wolyéé ńt’éé’ ’éí shį́į́ Chíí’ ’ayóigo bich’ooní ńt’éé’ lá
Translation: Hastiin ’Adiits’a’ii éí Hooghan Hóchxǫ́’í (Manuelito, N.M.)-de’ Bilagáana Dah Shizhóód wolyéé ńt’éé’ ’éí bik’is nizhóní nít’éé’.

English: [Finally]
Gold: Jó ’éí ’abáágago
Translation: Wónáásdóó

English: The two of them built the trading post at the place called Blue Clay Point.
Gold: ’Áko ’éí yaa ndilt’éego Bis Dootł’izh Deez’áhí hoolyéegi naalyéhé bá hooghan ’áhoolaa
Translation: Bis Dootł’izh Deez’áhí hoolyéegi naakigo naalyéhé bá hooghan ’áhoolyaa

English: It was in the Spring when they moved there.
Gold: Dąągo ’ákwii ni’níná
Translation: ’Íídą́ą́’ dąągo kodóó ni’níná

English: There was an epidemic in progress, and we now refer to it as "the time when the throat killed many."
Gold: Naałniih dinék’ehjígo hayaayááh dahóóghánę́ędą́ą́’ dabidii’ní k’ad
Translation: Ayóó ayáanii yilááh, k’ad éí ‘déé’ daats’į́’jí’ t’ą́ą́’ígíí nihił áníłtin.

English: It was at that time, in the spring, that they moved to Blue Clay Point, it was said.
Gold: ’Íídą́ą́’ dąągo t’ah ńt’éé’ Bis Dootł’izh Deez’áhí hoolyéegi ni’níná hodoo’niid
Translation: ’Íídą́ą́’ ’ákót’éego deesk’ą́ą́’go Bis Dootł’izh Deez’áhí hoolyéegi ninínáanii jiní

English: That is how it came about that the one who would be called The Interpreter (Chee Dodge) and the one who would be named Big Lump Setting Up came to move there.
Gold: K’adshą’ Hastiin ’Adiits’a’ii yidoolyeeł léi’ Dah Shizhóód yidoolyeeł léi’ kót’éego ’ákǫ́ǫ́ ninínáá lá
Translation: Kwe’é t’áá ’éí Hastiin ’Adiits’a’í yę́ę dooleełígíí dóó Łeeyitsoh ’Ałníí’í yę́ę dooleełígíí bighanahgóó deidiilnááh

English: They built the trading post and four years later perhaps, I do not recall exactly when, the one I called my uncle told us to haul wood there.
Gold: Naalyéhé bá hooghan ’áhoolyaa dóó dį́į́’ daats’í ’éí nááhaigo ’ákwii doo hazhó’ó bénáshniih da t’ah ńt’éé’ naalyéhé bá hooghandi chizh nihoheeh nihizhdííniid shidá’í ńt’éé’ dishnínígíí
Translation: Naalyéhé bá hooghan ’áhoolaa dóó dį́į́’ ha’ííná náádę́ę́’ daats’íí’, háádą́ą́’ doo t’áá shił bééhózin da, shidá’í ńt’éé’ dishnínígíí éí nihá ’áadi tsin ’ałnééhgo hádídziih

English: They (the traders) probably called for the wood.
Gold: ’Áádę́ę́’ shį́į́ chizh ho’doo’niidgo
Translation: ’Éíshą’ naalyéhé diné’é chizh yałníí’.

English: There was a boy of the Big Water Clan with whom I always chummed around.
Gold: ’Ashkii ła’ Tótsohnii nilį́įgo t’áá ’áłahjį’ bił tádísh’aash ’éí hoł
Translation: Ashkii léi’ Tótsohnii nilį́į́, shí bił t’áá jíík’ehgo naashá.

English: We started doing that kind of work.
Gold: ’Aadóó ’aají nihinaanish deezt’i’
Translation: ’Ákót’éego naanish nidiil’á.

English: We went about calling each other "younger brother,"
Gold: Sitsilí ’ahidii’níigo tádiit’aash
Translation: Shideezhí ’ałníí’ní́igo tádiit’aash

English: and we hauled wood to the trading post.
Gold: Naalyéhé bá hooghangi chizh nihiigeeh
Translation: ’Áádóó naalyéhé bá hooghan góó tsin nihidiiłnééł

English: We heard reports that there were people going about to get children put into school.
Gold: ’Áłchíní ’ólta’jį’ ndaha’níiłgo baa na’aldeeh jiní ha’níigo yii’nii’
Translation: ’íbąąs ha’níigo dine’é na’aldeehgo ’áłchíní ’ólta’góó ’adahat’ééshígíí ada’ííłį́

English: It was said that they were then over at Chinle,
Gold: Ch’ínílį́į́jí baa na’aldeeh jiní
Translation: ’Áko Chinlégi daalį́ jiní

English: and we heard that they were coming here sometime soon.
Gold: Hahgo shį́į́ kwii bił ’ínééh jiní ha’níigo yii’nii’
Translation: ’Áádóó t’áá íiyisí ’aadę́ę́’ ’oonééł ha’níigo nihinááł.

English: We would discuss it when we took the wagon after wood.
Gold: ’Áádóó baa yiníit’į́įgo chizh ha’iilbąąs
Translation: Tsinaabąąs bił chizh hanáánádááłgo, díí bee nihá daniyáłti’ lá.

English: "Say, let's go to school," I said to my companion.
Gold: ’Ashkihéi ’íídíiltah hodííniid hoł naash’aash yę́ę
Translation: ’Ólta’góó dii’níí’, shí bił hook’ee’ yiníłníí’.

English: "All right," he said.
Gold: Hágoshį́į́ jidííniid
Translation: Lą́’ąą ní jiní

English: And we went about, talking enthusiastically about it.
Gold: ’Aadóó baa yiníit’į́įgo baa nihił hózhǫ́ǫgo tádiit’aash
Translation: Dóó yá’át’ééhgo yee ’ałch’į’ nídiisdzíí’go t’áá ’áko danilwoł

English: In the evening after we had unloaded another load of wood we started back home in the wagon.
Gold: ’I’íí’ą́ągo chizh bida nááhee’nilgo hooghangóó dah ń’diilbą́ą́z
Translation: Tł’éé’honaa’éí, chizh t’áá ’ajį́ bidah ’ahii’nííłgo, tsinaabąs biyi’ t’óó hooghangóó nániikai.

English: When we got back to the hogan we found that my uncle was there.
Gold: Hooghandi nániit’áázh ńt’éé’ shidá’í yę́ę sidáá lá
Translation: Hooghangi nániikaigo ńt’éé’ shanáʼí sidá.

English: And it turned out that my grandfather, who was called Big Mexican Clansman, was there too.
Gold: Shichei Naakaii Dine’étsoh wolyéé ńt’éé’ ’éí dó’ sidáá lá
Translation: Áádóó áhoot’éego shichei yę́ę Naakaii Dine’étsoh wolyéé ’éíísh ’akwii nilį́.

English: So we told them of our plan.
Gold: ’Áko ’ákwe’é bee bił hwiilne’
Translation: ’Áko níhí nitsáhákees baa hwiilne’

English: "They are putting chidlren in school, it is said."
Gold: ’Áłchíní ’ólta’jį’ ndaha’nííł jiní
Translation: ’Áłchíní ’ólta’jį’ ndayiinííł jiní

English: We told them how we had both said, "Let's go to school."
Gold: T’áá ’áníidlah ’íídíiltah dii’niid dii’níigo bee hoł hwiilne’
Translation: Baa hane’ nihił yáłti’go, "’Ólta’góó dei’níłta’," níigo naaki nihí.

English: "It's probably all right.
Gold: T’áá shį́į́ ’áko
Translation: ’Éí shį́į́ t’áá shoodí

English: It's fine indeed, my children.
Gold: Yá’át’ééh lą́ą sha’áłchíní
Translation: T’áá íiyisí nizhóní, shiyázhí.

English: A party is in its way coming to us.
Gold: Jó ’aadę́ę́’ nihich’į’ ’oonééł lá
Translation: ’Íldee’ii nihá ’oonééł

English: You cannot escape them anyway," my uncle and my grandfather said to us.
Gold: Háadish dó’ baa dáádidooh’ash nihizhdííniid shidá’í yę́ę dóó shichei yę́ę
Translation: T’áá íiyisí doo bídáá’ dananishóód da, shidá’í dóó shicheii nihíł ní.

English: On the next day we went to the trading post, and my grandfather put his thumbprint on a paper for us.
Gold: Biiskání naalyéhé bá hooghangóó niikai dóó shichei yę́ę naaltsoos nihá bizhdeelchid
Translation: Náájígo naalyéhé bá hooghandi, dóó shichei nihá naaltsoos yidiilchił.

English: It was reported that the children from Chinle who were being taken to school would get there in two days, and we heard the grownups talking to one another about it.
Gold: Naaki yiską́ągo Ch’ínílį́į́dę́ę́’ ’áłchíní ’ólta’góó dadeesht’eezhígíí kwii bił ’íbąąs ha’níigo hastóí nihinááł yee ’ałch’į’ hadaasdzíí’
Translation: Yiską́ągo Ch’ínílį́déé’ ’áłchíní ’éí bina’nitin bighanigóó ndahaasht’eezhígíí naakigo déiyááł, dóó yee ’ałch’į’ hadaasdzíí’go hastóí nihí yisdá.

English: Of those menfolk who were talking to one another about it, one was called Weela. He lived over behind Round Rock
Gold: Yee ’ałch’į’ hadaasdzíi’ii hastóí ła’ Wéela wolyéé ńt’éé’ Tsénikání yine’jí kéédahat’į́į́ ńt’éé’
Translation: Baa na’níłní́ígíí hastóí biyi’ t’áá łá’ Wííla wolyé. Tsé Łichíí’ Dah ’Azkání biką’gi naagá.

English: and was one of the leaders at that time.

Gold: ’Akwii shichei ńt’éé’ nihee hajoodzíí’

English: Among those present were the men known as Black Horse, Limper, Tall Red House Clansman, Old Bead Chant Singer - who was of the Red House Clan - and his cousin, a Bitter Water Clansman called Bead Chant's Nephew, and another man with whom I was merely acquainted, and who was a relative of mine by marriage. Gold: Bilį́į́’ Łizhinii wolyéé ńt’éé’ Na’niłhodí wolyéé ńt’éé’ Kin Łichíi’nii Nééz wolyéé ńt’éé’ Yoo’ee Hataałí Sání wolyéé ńt’éé’ Kin Łichíi’nii nilį́įgo dóó bił naa’aash ńt’éé’ Tó Dích’íi’nii nilį́įgo Yoo’ee Bida’ wolyéé ńt’éé’ ła’ dó’ hastiin ńt’éé’ t’óó bééhasinígo bééhasin ńt’éé’ shá’áyééh ńt’éé’ ’li’di Aałiiłtsooí wolyéé ńt’éé’ k’ad t’áá ’ákódígo áádę́ę́’ yíkai yę́ę bénáshniih

Gold: ’Ako ’índa Haashch’ééłti’í ho’di’nínę́ę ’ak’ee’ąą hajííyá silį́į́’ ’Áko t’óó yikáihjí dah náhozhdiidlįįd jiní ’akon
Translation: Háálágo Haashchʼééłtiʼí wolyé éí ’ádiists’a’. Áádóó Ńléídi náá yá jiní

Gold: ’Aadóó baa ’áháyą́ągo t’áadoo hodíína’í neeyą́ jiní
Translation: Bee k’ehjígo ’awéé’ díkwíí’ nitsaa yį́į́’

English: Before the fourth day following that on which she was picked up, she could be sent on errands.
Gold: Názhníłtį́į́dóó dį́į́’ yiłkaah t’áá bich’į’ góne’ t’áadoo le’égóó naal’a’ silį́į́’
Translation: Bichxą́ą’ígííjį’ dį́į́’ íiyisígóó shádi’áádí, bina’anishgóó yidlą́ nít’éé’.

English: Something kept holding it down and she could not lift it up.

Translation: Díí yáłti’go atsiin yinéłts’ą́, ’áádóó Jóhonaa’éí dootł’izhii ajíí’ bikágíí dah si’ání ’áhoot’ééł.

English: So she knew that it must have been Sun who was holding down her wood.

Translation: Ha’át’íí ’éí łééchąą’í ndeił’inígíí?

English: I wondered what the dogs were barking at so I ran over there.
Gold: Ha’át’íí lá łééchąą’í ndeił’in lá nisingo ’áádóó ’ákǫ́ǫ́ ńdiishwod
Translation: Ha’át’íí lá łééchąą’í ndeił’in yiits’a’ yinísin dóó t’áá’ákwíí’ yę́ęgóó yishwoł

English: My cousin followed me.
Gold: Shił naa’aash dó’ t’áá shikéé’ joolwoł
Translation: Shił naa’aash shikéé’ déyá

English: I got over to where the dog was barking, and there I saw a bear standing.
Gold: Łééchąą’í ndahał’inę́ęjį’ yishwoł ńt’éé kǫ́ǫ́ shash sizį́įgo yiiłtsą́
Translation: Łééchąą’í ndeił’inígíí ’ákǫ́ǫ́ deeshááł, ’éí shash naaghá.

English: I stopped right there and looked at him.
Gold: T’áá ’áádóó ninishtłago t’áá ’áádóó nísh’į́
Translation: ’Áádę́ę́’ kojį’ nahásh’į́, bich’į’ naashnít.

English: He was really angry.
Gold: Hááhgóó shį́į́ báháchį’
Translation: Hááhgóó shį́į́ bee ak’ijį́’

English: He stood growling.
Gold: Biyi’ hodi’níigo sizį́
Translation: Yichxǫ́ǫ́hgo yizį́.

English: He was picking up things that were scattered on the ground about him, such as sticks and stones,
Gold: T’áadoo le’é ńléí tsin da ’akǫ́ǫ́ ndadeeztąądígíí tsé da náyiiláahgo yee ’adziiłne’
Translation: Kéyah bikáa’ dildę́ę́’go tsin dóó tsé t’áá ałtso naal’aah.

English: and threw them at the dogs.
Gold: Łééchąą’í yę́ę yee yitaa ’ałne’
Translation: ’Áádóó łééchąą’í baa yiilts’ą́.

English: He used sticks to strike among them
Gold: Tsin da yee yitaa’ałhaał
Translation: ’Atát’ah tsin bee yáyizéél

English: The dogs ran around him barking fiercely.
Gold: ’Áko hááhgóó shį́į́ łééchąą’í ndahał’ingo binánoodah
Translation: Łééchąą’í bik’id náádiit’ą́’go ts’ídágo ndahał’in.

English: I got that glimpse of him and then I dashed away.
Gold: T’óó ’ákót’éego bik’í níghal dóó yaashtáál
Translation: Navajo: Éí t’áá ’áłts’íís yíníł’į́, ’áko shínáádiilwod.

English: My cousin too lost no time in running away.
Gold: Shił naa’aash dó’ t’áá shikéé’ yajiiltáál
Translation: ’Ákwii łá t’áá jį́ yaa yíłchééł.

English: I stopped at a place far removed from the scene.
Gold: Ńléí doo deeghánídi ’índa ninishtła
Translation: ’Áádę́ę́’ ayóó déyáji’ diists’a’.

English: It was only after I stopped that my cousin caught up with me.
Gold: Ninishtłago ’índa ’áadi shíjílwod
Translation: T’áá shoodí shí náhást’éego, shił naa’aash shił náádiilnih.

English: Then we started off again, and went over to where the sheep were walking in order to get in ahead of them and cut them off.
Gold: ’Áadóó dah náádiit’ázhí ’éí ńléí dibé yikahą́ą bidááhjí ’iit’áázh
Translation: Nááji’ t’áá ni’ dah náádiikai dóó dibé danááhígíí dei’á, kót’éego biniiyé bi’ájígóó dei’á dóó hadínínááh.

English: We headed them off toward the flat.
Gold: ’Áádóó ’índa ńléí dzígaijigo dibé béé’niilnii’
Translation: Dzígaigóó niilkaad

English: We herded them back down to the open country.
Gold: ’Éí ńléí dah ńdzílgai léi’jį’ ch’ééní’niilkaad
Translation: Dibé ’áadi téehdi nináá’niilkaad.

English: We stayed down there and herded the sheep until noon.
Gold: ’Éí t’áá ’ákwii na’aniilkaadgo ’ałní’ní’ą́
Translation: ’Áadi téehdi dibé na’niilkaad abíní naakits’áadah ’ałní’áádgo jį́’

English: That is how I saw my first bear.
Gold: ’Íídą́ą́’ ’ákót’éego ts’ídá ’áłtsé shash yiiłtsą́ą ni’
Translation: ’Ákót’éego shash t’áá áłtségo shił nít’éé’ ni’

English: I saw another one on the following day, but at a distance, and walking on the mountainside.
Gold: Biiskání ła’ náánéiłtsą́ą ndi ’éí ńléí ’ákohdi t’áá nízaadi binániigi yigáał náánéiłtsą́
Translation: Hajį́’go la’í ’ákohdi dziłtát’ahgóó yiyáago shí yinish’ą́.

English: It turns out that must be a bear.
Gold: ’Ei ga’ ’óolyéé lá shash t’óó nisin
Translation: Shash lá ńt’éé’

English: In the fall of that same year we moved from the mountain back down into the valley to herd down there.
Gold: Náánáłah ’éiyá t’áá ’éidí bi’aak’eedi ’éi doo dziłghą́ą’di da ’éí t’áá ńléí téehdi ’áadi ninánii’náago nináá’niilkaad ńt’éé’
Translation: Díí t’áá íiyisí ak’ehgo, dziłdi tahdi ’adiiná; tahdi dibé na’ałkaah.

English: We had the rams in the herd, and they used to really fight with one another.
Gold: Deenásts’aa’ ’atah ndaakaigo bił na’aniilkaad
Translation: Dibé hastł’ó’í nihidibé bił hólǫ́, dóó t’áá yéego ’ałch’į’ na’aztł’ááh.

English: When the rams would attack and butt each other we would each get astride a ram and then urge them to attack.
Gold: ’Áko ńléí ła’ ’ałk’i náánéilwo’go da’ahógeehgo ’ałts’ą́ą́hjí bik’i dah nániikeehgo ’ałch’į’ nihił nínáhidí’níilchéeh łeh
Translation: Ńléí danáádiilwo’ dóó bitsiits’iin yee ná’oolchííhgo, t’áá’ t’áá’ át’éego ńléí bik’i dah siikéego, ’ádę́ę́’ danáádiilwo’ nihíji’ nisin.

English: We would sit on them, and when their heads came crashing together we would really die laughing.
Gold: Bik’i dah siikéego bitsiits’iin yee ná’ahiigohgo hááhgóó shį́į́ baa dlo nihighą́ą łeh ni’
Translation: Bik’i dah nihishą́, ’ałch’į’ náádiilwo’go t’áá ákót’éego baa dlo nihighą́ą łeh.

English: Some times we would fall off, and we would really laugh then too.
Gold: Łahda bidah ’anániidahgo hááhgóó shį́į́ baa dlo nihighą́ą łeh
Translation: ’Áádę́ę́’ bidah dadiijihgo dóó hááhgóó shį́į́ baa dlo íiyisí łeh ni’

English: That is how we used to have fun with the rams.
Gold: Kót’éego deenásts’aa’ bee nei’née łeh ni’
Translation: ’Áko ’ákót’éego dibé ba’áádé’éłígíí bił nei’niná łah ńt’éé’

English: Sometimes the rams would get far apart and my cousin would step in between them and then jump aside as their heads came together.
Gold: Łahda ńléí doo deeghánídę́ę́’ deenásts’aa’ ’ałts’ą́ą́’ ninát’ashgo ’aadę́ę́’ ’ałch’į’ náádiilwo’go bita’ góne’ ’aníjílwo’go t’áá ’ahánídę́ę́’ ’ahinoolchéełgo ’índa níláahjį’ ch’ééjiilyeedgo kót’éego da baa neit’aash łeh ńt’éé’
Translation: Łahgo ’ałk’í ayóo náádiilnááhgo, shí ’ak’éí bináji’ yááh, ’áko bitsiits’iin yee ná’ahiigohgo yájíłjáá’.

English: The sheep would be grazing nearby, and we would spend the whole day playing with the rams.
Gold: Dibé t’óó nihiná náákahgo shábíighah deenásts’aa’ bee nei’née łeh ni’
Translation: Dibé nihikǫ́’go tł’oh yiyiiyááł, dóó jį́ t’áá iiyisí dibé hastł’į́í bił na’oolkaah.

English: Once we had billy goats in the herd.
Gold: Tł’ízí chǫǫh dó’ ’atahgo bił na’niilkaad ńt’éé’ łah
Translation: Tł’ízí ką’ bił na’aniilkaad łah ńt’éé’

English: That took place down on the plain too,
Gold: ’Éí ’ałdó’ t’áá ńléí halgaidi
Translation: Łahda bikáa’gi íiyisí ’áhóót’įįd.

English: not in the mountains.
Gold: Doo dziłdi da
Translation: Doo dziłghą́ą’di da.

English: We had one billy goat in the herd that was just a little bit mean.
Gold: Tł’ízí ką’ ła’ t’áá bíyó hashkéego bił na’niilkaad ńt’éé’
Translation: Tł’ízí chǫǫh t’áá łá’í t’áá bíyó yéé’ ’ats’áadahígíí ’atahgo bił na’niilkaad

English: If a person would bother him, like pinching him or walking behind him, he would get mad.
Gold: ’Áko ńléí ha’át’éegi da baa níjít’įįhgo bí’dzíts’ihgo bikéé’jígo jidigháahgo da hach’į’ báháchįįh
Translation: Diné t’ááłá’í éí yich’į’go, t’áá ákwíí’ yits’ós dóó yíká nahgáá’ígíí, éí yilá.

English: We always herded sheep with a burro, sitting one behind the other.
Gold: ’Áko díí t’áá ’áłahjį’ télii bee na’niilkaad ’ałkéé’ dah siikéego
Translation: T’áá íiyisí télíí bił dibé baa nanináh, kojigo ’ałkéé’ bikáá’ nisdááh.

English: But when one would be riding the burro the billy goat would merely look up if one teased him.
Gold: ’Éí bikáá’dóó baa níjít’į́įgo ’éí ’áłtąą t’óó náhoníl’įįh łeh
Translation: ’Ał’ą́ą́’ télii ba’ííníidlíigo, bá yiiyááłgo bine’jí t’áá íiyisí dah yilá.

English: He wouldn't do anything under these circumstances even if one got very close to him.
Gold: ’Ákót’éego dó t’éiyá t’áá ’áháníjį’ bit’áahjį’ na’adá
Translation: Díí bik’ehgo, índa łá’ bich’į’ náájíigo déyááł, éí doo t’áá íiyisíí yá’áhoot’ééł da.

English: But the minute you dismounted in front of him, he came for you.
Gold: Bich’į’ bidajigháahgo ’éí t’áá ’áko hach’į’ nídiilwo’
Translation: ’Índa t’áá íiyisí bich’į’ nidajíí’ágo, níyá.

English: That is how we used to herd sheep when this dangerous billy goat was present.
Gold: ’Áko ’ákót’éego tł’ízí ką’ doo baa náhát’į́į́góó bił na’aniilkaad łah ńt’éé’
Translation: Kót’éego dibé na’niilkaad díí hashkéí tł’ízí hastínígíí bika’go.

English: One time we got to wondering what he might do to us. He was grazing at a distance, and we went up to him on the burro.
Gold: Aadóó łah ’ííshją́ą́’ shį́į́ daa nihizhdoolííł dii’níigo ńléí ’ákohdi naagháago na’ałchozhgo ’ákǫ́ǫ́ bich’į’ télii nihił yílwod
Translation: T’áá íiyisí nihínízin, ‘Ha’át’íí nihá nít’į́į́?’ T’áá nízaadígíí tł’oh yiyá, dóó básóóz biką’ dah daniidlį́’go ’éí baa danááh.

English: When we got there I dismounted right in front of him.
Gold: ’Áádóó shí bich’į’ bidéíyá
Translation: K’ad deiiyáago shí bich’į’ t’áá ’áádóó bidajighááh.

English: I went up behind him, and he wheeled around to face me.
Gold: Kojígo bitł’aayahjígo déyáá ńt’éé’ shich’į’ náhaastah
Translation: Bikéé’jígo naashá dóó shich’į’ nikináánádzá

English: Then he started trotting toward me,
Gold: Dóó ’aadę́ę́’ shich’į’ nikeeldloozh
Translation: ’Aadóó shich’į’ dah nízdeesk’ą́ą́’

English: so I ran over behind the burro.
Gold: ’Aadóó dah diishwod dóó télii bine’jígo ’eeshwod
Translation: ’Áádóó télii bine’jígo ’ákǫ́ǫ́ ńdiishwod

English: Then my cousin, with whom I was herding sheep, jumped off the burro too.
Gold: Shił naa’aash hoł na’nishkaadę́ę dó’ bidah yajiiltáál
Translation: ’Áko dibé bił shí na’nishkaadígíí shiyázhí éí da bóóro bikáá’di yááts’ááh.

English: He approached the goat that was chasing me and it ran toward him.
Gold: Tł’ízí ką’ náshidíníiłchą́’ą́ą bich’į’ nikizhníyáá ńt’éé’ ’aadę́ę́’ hach’į’ nínáádiilwod
Translation: Shí yidiilwodígíí’ hach’į’ yaa níyá dóó bíyáá’ dah diilwod.

English: The goat went for him, but just before it could hit him he jumped outside and the goat went on past him.
Gold: Hach’į’ dah diilwodgo t’áá ’íiyisíí t’áá ła’ hoolaago bidinínáajigo ’ádee’iijoolghaalgo t’óó hwííghahgóó ch’élwod
Translation: Tł’ízí bá yich’į’, t’áá sháá’ ts’ídá ’ahinoolch’éeł, ’ádóó tł’ízí yinaał’į́’.

English: The goat went a little distance, turned around and came for us again.
Gold: Nagháí ’ákohdi naanáswodgo ’áádę́ę́’ nihich’į’ nikináánádzá
Translation: Tł’ízí haa shį́į́ íiyisí nízahjį’, dah nízhdiidzá, ’áádę́ę́’ niháá’ yá.

English: The faithful burro that we rode was now behind the billy goat.
Gold: Télii ba’ííníidlíigo nanihiyéhę́ę ’éí níwohjígo bine’jígo sizį́
Translation: ’Éí télii nihí bikáá’dóó baa níjít’į́į’ígíí baa hwiinídzinígíí náádi tł’ízí ką’ binaagóó ’áhoot’é

English: So we ran in the direction opposite the burro,
Gold: ’Aadóó t’óó bits’ą́ąjigo ’ahaa dah diit’áázh
Translation: Áko búróó bits’áadahgóó nániichééł.

English: and the goat trotted along behind us.
Gold: ’Aadóó nihikéé’ nikeeldloozh
Translation: Dóó tł’ízí nihikéé’ yildlosh.

English: He was driving us away from the burro.
Gold: Télii yę́ę yits’ą́ąjigo nihidínéeshchą́ą́’
Translation: Télii bidááhgo nihinaaznil.

English: We kept right on running ahead of him, with him trotting along behind us.
Gold: Ts’ídá t’ááłáhági ’át’éego bilą́ąjį’ ’ahaa yiit’ash nihikéé’ yildloshgo
Translation: ’Áádóó bí yáájáádgo t’áá jí náádideeshwoł, nihikéé’ éí nikeeldloozh.

English: We were running in the direction of home, which lay about three miles away.
Gold: Táadi tsin sitą́ądi daats’í nihighango ’áajigo nániichééł
Translation: Díí shádi’go t’áá íiyisí táá’ mííl nihí hooghanjigo ’ahaa dah diit’áázh.

English: We got to a little hill near home, on which there were some outcroppings of rock.
Gold: Hooghan t’áá ’áhání hadziihgo nagháí ’át’éegi t’áá ’áłts’íísígo tsé bił dah yisk’idgo ’ákwii tsé hadaazt’i’go ’éí bíhi’niilchą́ą́’
Translation: Hooghan bits’áádę́ę’ t’áá ’áhoołts’íísígi dził nídeiyá, bikáa’gi tsé da nidishgiizhí.

English: There we crawled into a little niche in the rock.
Gold: ’Ákwii t’áá ’áhoołts’íísígo tsétł’ááh léi’ góne’ ’ii’na’
Translation: ’Éí tsé bits’ósí yázhí biyi’ yáshjaa’.

English: The goat came right up to the opening,
Gold: ’Áajį’ tł’ízí ką’ nihidaníyá
Translation: Nagháí t’áá íiyisí daaztsʼáʼ bíyááʼ náháníłʼą́

English: as we lay there in the space beneath the rock.
Gold: Tséyaa góne’ shiitéezhgo
Translation: Tsé bits’áá’ góne’ ’ákwii danihíyágo.

English: He took his spite out on the rock, butting it,
Gold: Hááhgóó shį́į́ ch’ééh tsé néinigoh
Translation: Yizhdáhgo tsé naayijįʼ

English: and bit at our feet,
Gold: Wónáásdóó hááhgóó shį́į́ nihikee’ yółháásh
Translation: Dóó nihikéé’ yixxǫ́ǫ́’

English: He did every thing he could think of, in an effort to get us out, while we just lay there kicking at him.
Gold: Hááhgóó shį́į́ bíighahí ’ánihooł’įįłgo nihidáádinízį́
Translation: Nihí náájiil’ááh nisinígíí biniiyé’ t’áá íiyisí áyóo hodidoołnih, t’áá nít’į́į́’go t’áá jiyáádgo éí bił na’al’į́į́’.

English: My cousin told me not to bother him, to just keep quiet and lie still, so we just lay still.
Gold: Nihí ’éi kodóó t’óó ’áhodínílzéé’ t’áadoo nahí’nání sínítį́ shijiníigo t’áadoo nahii’nání shiitéézh
Translation: Shił naa’aash ’áshijiní doo bá nídoodleeł da, háálá dóó t’áá hajíínóonííł, ’áko nihí t’áá hajíínóonid.

English: The goat tired in his efforts to get us so he calmed down too,
Gold: Ch’éé ’ánihííł’įįdgo bídó’ t’óó ’áhodiilzee’
Translation: Nagháí nihich’į’ nikináánáígíí biniinaa ’ádíní́, éí shoodí naahalin.

English: and just stood there watching us.
Gold: T’óó nihésį́
Translation: ’Aadóó nihí yit’ááhgo t’óó naazį́

English: After a long time the goat went away.
Gold: Daashį́į́ nízah nihoolzhiizhgo níwohjį’ dah diiyá
Translation: Yiską́ągo tł’ízí ’ííyá

English: The Sun had just gone down,
Gold: ’Áko ńléí góyaa ’i’íí’ą́
Translation: Jóhonaa’éí jį́ʼ hwiitʼááh.

English: and as soon as the goat went away we crawled back out of the hole.
Gold: Tł’ízí chǫǫh yę́ę ’ííyáago ’índa tsétł’ááhdę́ę́’ háásii’na’
Translation: Áádóó nagháí dah diiyágo t’áá shoodí kǫ’góne’ náá dánichxį́į́’.

English: We could see him going along homeward.
Gold: T’óó níil’į́įgo hooghan yich’į’go náádááł
Translation: Bíhooghanahgóó yilwo’ yinééł

English: So we followed him back home.
Gold: ’Aadóó ńléí hooghandi bikéé’ ná’ahininiilchą́ą́’
Translation: ’Aádóó bihooghanáá’góó bí náániikai

English: Fortunately all the sheep had returned,
Gold: Ńt’éé’ t’áá shǫǫ dibéhę́ę t’áá ’ałtso nákai lá ’ałdó’
Translation: Yá’át’ééhgo dibé t’áá ałtso nínáánih

English: as well as the burro.
Gold: Télii yę́ę da
Translation: Télii té’é’į́ ’akon

English: We went about the task of milking goats for our supper.
Gold: ’Aadóó ’átsą́ ’ídi’diilnííł biniiyé ’ii’nihgo baa nídiit’áázh

English: My cousin did the milking,
Gold: Shił naa’aash ’éí ní’jii’nih
Translation: Shił naa’aash béégashii yíłchoozh.

English: while usually held the goat's head for him.
Gold: Shí ’éí t’óó há ’atsii’ yíníshtą’ łeh
Translation: Éí ádį́ą́ą́ biniiyé tł’ízí bitsii’ yijoolgo.

English: That was my job.
Gold: ’Ákwe’é t’éiyá bee choosh’į́į łeh
Translation: Shina’anish nít’į́.

English: While we were doing our milking this old goat that had chased us all over the place got mad at us again.
Gold: ’Áko ’ákwe’é ’iinihgo baa neit’aash ńt’éé’ díí tł’ízí chǫǫh nanihineeshchą́’ą́ą t’áá ’éí nihich’į’ bánááhóóchįįd
Translation: Tł’ízí bitoo’ deiilts’íísgo díí tł’ízí ts’óózí nihí baa nááh dah ’iłníí’ígíí náá nihik’ehgo hashké yíłts’ą́.

English: He suddenly came for us from a place close by.
Gold: T’áadoo hooyání t’áá ’áhánídę́ę’ nihich’į’ ch’elwod
Translation: T’ah ńt’éé’ góne’ shį́į́ nihich’į’ nikinááná

English: I saw him coming, but before I could turn he butted me in the hip and knocked me down.
Gold: T’áá yiiłtsą́ą ndi t’áadoo disyésí díí shik’ai’ góne’ yizgoh dóó naa’ashídzíígo’
Translation: Yááłígíí shíníł’į́, t’áá íiyisí shinaniná’go shijáád shidiilwod dóó shigha’ yíts’į́.

English: My legs went up in the air and one of my moccasins fell off and went flying.
Gold: Shijáád yáániidee’go kélchí shikee’ ńt’éé’ shaa diilts’idgo ńléí dego yanáaltáál

Translation: Ts’ídá shich’į’ nínáádiilwodgo Gogo yéékeedgo hayaadóó haalwod dóó shich’į’ yisdloh jiní

English: I was frightened to death.
Gold: ’Áádóó t’óó báhádzidígi ’át’éego nísísdzííd
Translation: T’áá jíík’eh yishjool

English: I started running and the dog right after me.
Gold: ’Aadóó dah diishwod łééchąą’í yę́ę t’áá shikéé’ dah diilwod
Translation: Yiit’ash nishááh dóó łééchąą’í t’ááłáhági shikéé’ yildlosh

English: From the distance I kept my eye on our things.
Gold: T’óó t’áá ńléí ’ákohdę́ę́’ héłę́ę nísh’į́
Translation: Ńléígóó nihit’į́į́’ baa hályą́́

English: And then another coyote attacked me from another side.
Gold: Ńt’éé’ náánáłahdę́ę’go mą’ii ła’ shich’į’ nínáádiilwod
Translation: Áko t’áá łá’ mą’ii t’éiyágo shaa tiih

English: Just as this one jumped on me the dog came to my rescue,
Gold: T’áá łá’ nááshiidlaago łééchąą’í shíká ’anáánáálwod
Translation: Ts’ídá t’áá ła’ díí shinaaghaałgo łééchąą’í ’áajį’ shá dah yiite’

English: and drove that one off too.
Gold: Shik’inéiinííłchą́ą́’
Translation: Dóó ’éí náá nííłchą́ą́’.

English: That is how the dog protected me.
Gold: ’Ákót’éego łééchąą’í shich’ą́ą́h naayáa ni’
Translation: ’Éí łééchąą’í shí ’ííyá nisingo

English: Now as think about it, it is a good thing to have a dog.
Gold: ’Áko k’ad ’íinisingo t’áá ’ákónéehee łééchąą’í hwee hólǫ́ǫ łeh lá
Translation: Ndí shí éí nítsékeesgo, łééchąą’í hólǫ́ígíí yá’át’ééh.

English: A dog can save one's life.
Gold: T’áá bine’ dzidoodzihgo haz’ą́ą́ lá ’akon
Translation: Łééchąą’í t’áá hach’ą́ą́h haz’ą́ą́.

English: I still remember my dog.
Gold: ’Éidíígíí beego shilééchąą’í t’ah bénáshniih
Translation: Shilééchąą’í t’ah bénáshniih

English: I don't forget him,
Gold: Doo baa yooshnéeh da
Translation: Doo bíshdaalnih da.

English: because he protected me.
Gold: Shich’ą́ą́h ’ííyá nisingo
Translation: Shich’ą́ą́h naayáago biniinaa

English: A dog will save a person when he is alone without protection.
Gold: Ha’át’éegi da t’áá sáhá bił niji’aashgo t’áá hach’ą́ą́h ’adoogáałgo haz’ą́ą́ lá
Translation: Łééchąą’í t’áá íiyisígo diné yinaaznil

English: I found that out.
Gold: ’Éí ’ákót’éego shił bééhózin
Translation: Shíł béédahoozin

English: It was about a year after that a lot of people died.
Gold: ’Áádóó náhodeeshzhiizhí ’éí t’ááłá’í daats’í t’áá ’éí nínáánááhaigo ’ádahasdįįd ni’
Translation: ’Áko t’ááłáʼí níłchʼitsoh yę́ędą́ą́go diné lą’í dabííghą́.

English: The white people say that it was in 1918.
Gold: ’Éí Bilagáanají 1918 yę́ędą́ą́’ ’ádahasdįįd daaní
Translation: 1918 bits’ą́ą́’ át’é Bilagáana yíníłtiʼ.

English: It was at that time that people died from an epidemic of influenza.
Gold: ’Íídą́ą́’ ’ákót’éego tah honiigááh diné dabííghą́ ’akon
Translation: ’Íídą́ą́’ hayaayááh naałniih biniinaa diné ’ádahasdįįd

English: In some places whole families died.
Gold: Łahgóó t’áá dahooghan ńt’éé’ ’ádahasdįįd ni’
Translation: Łahgóó bighan biyi’ dine’é t’áá ałtso doo nít’į́ da.

English: In other places just a few survived.
Gold: Łahgóó t’áá díkwíhí dadzoodzíí’
Translation: Łah ’áłdáádi góó t’áá áłts’íísí danilééh.

English: I had a hard time during that period.
Gold: Shí ’éí ’ákwe’é shich’į’ ninááhwiis’náá’
Translation: ’Akót’į́į́’go ’atah shich’į’ nahwiis’náa ni’

English: I used to have some brothers and sisters.
Gold: Bił háíjéé’ danilíinii hólǫ́ǫ́ ńt’éé’
Translation: Shideezhí dóó shinaaí dóó shádí ła’ da dahólǫ́ ni’

English: There were nine of us.  I was the ninth.
Gold: Náhast’éí ńt’éé’
Translation: Náhást’éí daniilį́. Shí náhást’éí nishłį́.

English: Eight of us died.
Gold: Tseebíí ’éí ’ádaadin daazlį́į́’
Translation: Nihá tseebíí ’ádahasdįįd ni’

English: I just barely pulled through.
Gold: Shí t’éiyá hojoobá’ígo ch’í’ííłdįįd
Translation: Shí t’áá ’áłts’íísgo shį́į́ haayáá.

English: I had a hard time during the flu epidemic.
Gold: Tah honiigááh diné bitaadaasnii’go ’atah shich’į’ nahwiis’náa ni’
Translation: Hayaayááh naałniihgi shich’į’ ninááhwiis’náá’.

English: At that time there were no doctors nearby.
Gold: ’Íídą́ą́ ’éí t’áá ’áhánígi ’azee’ííł’íní ’ádaadin
Translation: ’Íídą́ą́’ bidiʼááh ’azee’ dineʼé doo dahólǫ́ da.

English: Probably the only hospital then was the one at Fort Defiance,
Gold: Ńléí Tséhootsooídi shį́į́ t’éiyá ’azee’ál’į́ ’íídą́ą́’
Translation: Háálá ’adę́ę́’ t’áá łá íiyisí ’azee’ ’áhoot’į́í éí Tséhootsooígi ’át’é.

English: and possible the one at Ganado.
Gold: Kojí Lók’aah Nteeljí shį́į́ ’ałdó’
Translation: ’Aádóó t’éiyá Lók’aah Nteeldi ’azee’ál’į́ ’éí.

English: Just very recently some hospitals were built, but we do not have enough of them.
Gold: Jó k’ad ’éiyá t’áá ’ádíyídígo ’azee’ál’į́ ’ádaalyaa ndi t’áá nihi’oh dahonee’ą́ ’akon
Translation: T’áá ’ániidígo ’azee’ál’į́įd ’áłts’áá’ si’ání, ’ádóó doo nihí níłts’ą́ą’ da.

English: As a result, when people got sick they really suffered everywhere.
Gold: Jó ’ákót’éego diné bąąh dah dahoo’a’go diné t’áá ’íiyisíí ti’dahooznii’ ni’ daałahgóó
Translation: Ákót’éego, diné doo yá’át’ééh daago t’áá níłtéél yéigo ’adáhoot’ééł.

English: Back then that was how I suffered among others.
Gold: Shí ’ákót’éego ’atah shich’į’ nahwiis’náa’ ni’ ’íídą́ą́’
Translation: Háálá t’áá ’ákót’é shí łáá’ bił bee’eldǫǫdígíí shidahooznii’ jiní

English: I have told the things that happened when I was a boy. I'm telling it to you children.
Gold: Díí k’ad ńléí ’ashkii nishłį́į́dą́ą́’ ’ádahóót’įįdii t’áá béédaashniihígi bee ’ádaa hashne’
Translation: Ashkii yázhígo ’ádahóót’įįdii bee nihił nahosisne’. Áłchíní, bee nihił nahosisne’.

English: Some of you children have mothers and fathers who are living.
Gold: Jó díí ’áłchíní danohłíinii ła’ nihimá ’índa nihizhé’é da dahólǫ́
Translation: Ła’ ’éí ’áłchíní t’áá shoodí nihimá dóó nihizhé’é hólǫ́.

English: Some of your mothers are not living.
Gold: Ła’ ’éí nihimá ’ádaadin
Translation: Jó nihimá ła’ doo dahólǫ́ da.

English: But even so, don't forget your parents.
Gold: Ndi ’áko ndanihiishchíinii doo baa dayoohnééhgóó béédaałniih

English: I am saying so.
Gold: ’Áko ’ádíshní ’akon
Translation: ’Ákót’éego yáníłti’.

English: Sometimes a child gets into mischief and doesn't mind his mother.
Gold: ’Áłchíní jílį́įgo t’áá ni’dziisíih ndi łahgóó hamá doo bik’eh hojíł’į́į́góó łahda ’anáá’át’ááh
Translation: Łahda ’awéé’ ts’ídá ’ádaanííł dóó doo amá bił yínínééh da.

English: Even so, he gets wiser and wiser. His mind grows and strengthens,
Gold: Jó ’áko ndi t’áá hojooyąął t’áá háni’ hooleełgo t’áá háni’ yiłdził
Translation: ’Áko t’áá íiyisí nitsáhákees yá’át’ééhgo nááda’diilyaa. Bínitsáhákees yich’į’ dóó yilts’ą́.

English: and when he is told to do something he knows what to do.
Gold: Ha’át’íi da bich’į’ ho’dil’áá shį́į́ t’áá yéego baa ’áhozhniizįįh
Translation: ’Áko ha’át’íí íiyisí baa nilne’go, ha’át’íí íiyisí bééhózin.

English: As time goes on, a child develops his thinking from his mother and father.
Gold: Wónáásdóó ntsáhákeesígíí t’áá hó hazhé’é ’índa hamá da bits’ą́ą́dóó hwee hooleeł

English: That's the Navajo way.
Gold: Jó kót’éego ’éí dinéjí ’iiná
Translation: Éí Diné binahagha’

English: That's the way children grow up.
Gold: ’Éí ’áájí ’ákót’éego jiinaah
Translation: Kót’éego ’áłchíní yá’áhoot’ééł

English: His grandparents are like teachers to him. He asks them how The People used to live, and they tell him.
Gold: Hachaii da nayízhdíłkidgo hanálí da nayízhdíłkidgo hamá sání da ńléidą́ą́ yik’ehgo dayíkaii ’índa badahane’ da danilíinii ’éí bázhdiits’a’go ’ákót’éego bá ’ajółta’ nahalin
Translation: Bicheii dóó binálí éí bił naʼaahígíí ’át’é. Diné haash yiní kéédahwiit’į́į́ bá yinaahkʼid, dóó bił yáłtiʼ.

English: It is akin to the textbooks of the white people.
Gold: T’áá kojí Bilagáanají naaltsoos yits’ą́ą́dóó ’ídahooł’aahígi ’át’éego
Translation: ’Éí Bilagáana bináaltsoos bąąh dah na’aznilígíí ’áhoot’éego.

English: It is said that, in the past, the people really made it a point to teach one another.
Gold: T’ah nahdę́ę́’ diné t’áá yéego nda’ahinitin ńt’éé’ daaní
Translation: ’Áłk’idą́ą́’ jiní, Diné’é yéego bá na’ólta’ jiní

English: But today we are lax and do not teach our children much.
Gold: Yéego na’anitin yee ’ałch’į’ yádaalti’go kót’éego ła’ tsíłkéí yá’át’éhgo biyaa dahoo’a’
Translation: Dííjį́ ndi doo nihina’nitin baa nitsídilééh da, dóó doo t’áá íiyisí nihá’áłchíní nidanitin da.

English: Some of us neglect our children.
Gold: Jó k’ad dííjį́ ’éiyá t’óó ’ahídayíníilkáá’ nahalingo naha’áłchíní łahgóó doo hózhǫ́ ndaniitin da
Translation: T’áá ła’íí éí niha’áłchíní doo baa nitsíkees da

English: We somewhat don’t think for our children.
Gold: T’áá bíyó ła’ niha’áłchíní doo hózhǫ́ bá ntsídeiikees da ’akon

English: It’s well doable for us to teach our children those things
Gold: Jó ’éidíígí hazhó’ó niha’áłchíní ndaniitingo yá’át’ééh t’áá ’ííghah

English: Even though your children are taught for you in school, we should not lose sight of our teaching.
Gold: Nihá nanitin dadohníi ndi jó ’akon jó t’áá nihí nihina’nitin ’ałdó’ t’áá ’óóltą’go yá’át’ééh shidine’é ’ałtah ’áásįįłóó
Translation: Łahgo nihí ’áłchíní ’ólta’gi baa noosdzááh, nihina’nitin doo nidiits’a’ da.

English: I am now telling these stories of mine to your children.
Gold: Díidíígíí shahane’ígíí k’ad nizhónígo ’áłchíníkǫ́ǫ́ bee bił ndahashne’
Translation: Díí k’ad díí shihaneʼé ni’áłchíní baa nishneʼ.

English: Thes stories that you heard are those that I remember happening when I was a child.
Gold: T’áá díkwíígóó shį́į́ dii ńléí ’áłchíní ’ídlį́į́dą́ą́’ ’ádahóót’įįdii t’áá bénáshniihígi shá dasidoots’ą́ą́’
Translation: Díí haneʼ níníłígíí ’éiyá shiyázhígo ’ádahóót’įįdii shijólta’.

English: So then it’s good that one recalls those stories, those things that happened. That’s how you have memories.
Gold: ’Áko yá’át’ééh ’ákót’éego ńléídę́ę́’ dahane’ danilíinii yę́ę ’índa łahgóó ’ádahóót’įįdii nát’ą́ą́’ hoł níjólta’go jó ’áko ’éí bee háni’ hooleeł łeh ’akon
Translation: Áko yá’át’ééh hané’ dóó ńléí ’ádahóót’įįdii náhodíílnih. T’áá éiyá éí níhodíílnih.

English: That’s how you strenghten your mind.
Gold: ’Éí bee háni’ yiłdzil łeh lá ’akon
Translation: T’áá ’áko nitsáhákees yiłdził.

English: Back in the beginning we lived without knowledge of our leaders (i.e. the Government, President, Commissioner, etc.)
Gold: Kwe’é díí bee hahóóyáádą́ą́’ nihinant’a’í doo nihił bééhózingóó kééhwiit’į́į́ ńt’éé’
Translation: T’áá íiyisígo nihinaat’áanii bee doo bééhózin da.

English: To the President in Washington and the officials under him, to the government officials all the way from Washington down to Window Rock, to the Tribal Council Officers and to the members of the Council, to the Chapter Officers, the womenfolk and the youths, to all those who know what trouble is, we are telling about problems and asking them to give these matters their consideration.
Gold: K’ad ’éí díí ha’a’aahdi Wááshindoondi ’alą́ąji’ naat’áanii jílínígíí ’índa hakéé’ góne’ sinilígíí t’áá ’át’é dóó Tségháhoodzáníjį’ ’adíítąądii ’áádóó wóshdę́ę́’ díí k’ad t’áá ’ałtso kodi nihinant’a’í béésh bąąh dah naaz’ání yá dah sikéii dóó wóshdę́ę́’ ’índa béésh bąąh dah si’ání t’áá ’ałtso dóó hastóí táá’ naaznilí ha’níinii ’áádóó sáanii ’índa tsíłkéí siih nízinii t’áá ’ałtso ńdeikąąhgo díí niha’áni’ danilíinii nihahane’ danilíinii hazhó’ó bee nihił ndahodiilnih nisingo ’ádíshní
Translation: Wááshindoondi Naat’áanii dóó bidá’ah naat’áanii, Wááshindoon nitsaaígíí t’áá deidiit’ááhgo Tségháhoodzánígóó t’áá ałtso bee haz’ą́anii dine’é, Naachid naat’áanii dóó Naachid biyi’ danilį́į́’, Chaptá naat’áanii, sáanii dóó ashkii dóó at’ééd yázhí, dóó doo yá’át’ééh da át’éego bééhózinígíí t’áá ałtso góó, díí nihit’į́į́’ baa nihane’ dóó díí baa nídahooł’áah nitsékeesgo.

English: In the matter of what was done to livestock, they began these activities with the goats.
Gold: Kodóó díí k’ad dibé bee nihaa na’aldeeh bee nihaa ní’diildee’ dishnínígíí jó ’ałtsé tł’ízí bee nihaa na’asdee’
Translation: Dibé dóó tł’ízí bee hadadoonee’ígíí biniyé, díí naalnish tł’ízí bits’ą́ą’ t’áá ’áłts’íísgo náhoodleeł.

English: The womenfolk and children wept for their goats.
Gold: ’Áadóó sáanii yaa náácha ’áłchíní yaa dáácha
Translation: Sáanii dóó ’áłchíní bítłʼizí baa yicha’.

English: The bleating of the milk goats that fed the children faded away into the distance, and the wails of the children arose in their stead -- the wails of the children and the womenfolk.
Gold: ’Áłchíní bá ńdei’nih yę́ę nahgóó bicha’ ’adahididlaadgo kodóó dó’ ’áłchíní yázhí yaa cha hayííłne’ sáanii cha hayííłne’
Translation: ’Áłchíní yiyá tłʼízígíí yizééłí yádiłhiłgo deest’į́į́’, dóó bił dah ’áłchíní yichí’į’ hadaasdzíí’, ’áłchíní dóó sáanii yichí’į’.

English: They did not weep without reason, for the food of the people had been taken from them.
Gold: T’áá ’ákónéehee ’ádazhdííniid háálá diné bich’iyą’ yę́ę bighaalyá
Translation: Navajo: Doo íiyisí yishááh da, diné chʼiyáán kʼad binaʼ doo hólǫ́ da biniiyé.

English: It happened thus.
Gold: Kót’é
Translation: Kódzaa

English: Thereupon the police became active, and chaos reigned.
Gold: ’Ákwiidí kwii doo ’asohodéébéézhgóó kwii siláago ńdíníidaa’
Translation: ’Áko siláago yéego nayiisnish, dóó anáhóót’į́ náhoodleeł.

English: Our leaders, and those of us who failed to comply with orders to reduce our livestock, or who did not want the Special Grazing Regulations were told that we would be put in jail.
Gold: Naaltsoos bąąh dah łichí’ígíí doo nohsinii bi’oh ’íná’ídlééh danihi’di’nínígíí doo bida’ół’íinii ’aadóó diné bá yádaałti’ii díí t’áá’ánółtso yah ’adanihi’dii’níił dooleeł nihi’doo’niid
Translation: Nihí naat’áanii dóó nihí dibé dóó tł’ízí doo ná’azdzíh da’ígíí, áádóó Naałniih Bee Haz’ą́anii doo nihoníínízin da’ígíí, bighándę́ę́’ nihinááznil dooleeł nít’ę́ę́’ daanííłį́’.

English: We were told that any of us who spoke against the program would go to jail.
Gold: T’áá ha’át’éhégo da haahdzíi’ii t’áá ’ánółtso ’awáálya dooleeł nihi’doo’niid
Translation: Bee bík’eh dah naaznilígíí biká’ adiłhił danihi’ígíí yah ’adanihi’dii’níił dooleeł nihi’doo’niid

English: I still carry these thoughts in my mind.
Gold: ’Éí baa ntséskees t’óó
Translation: Ádęę’ díí nitsékees shijáádéé’ hólǫ́.

English: It is something akin to the dictatorial systems of government across the sea.
Gold: Díí la’ ńléí tónteel yónaaníjí hoot’áałii ’át’é
Translation: ’Éí tónteel yónaanídi beehaz’ání t’áá ’ée’ bee naat’áanii yádoołtéego danits’ą́’ígíí t’áá ’áhoot’éego át’é.

English: We hear stories to the effect that, in those areas, anyone who speaks unfavorably about the Government is killed. That's where we're headed.
Gold: ’Éí ’áájí ’éí t’áá doo zhǫ̨ǫdígo diné haadzihgo biniinaa kwiinahozhdisha dooleeł
Translation: Dahane’ danilíinii nihił hahoolyá jiní, ’éí bikéyahdi Sila béehaz’ą́ígíí t’áá íiyisí yisxí’go yiilaa’ jiní. ’Éídi nah wónaanígóó nidaashááł.

English: Why should anyone be manhandled just because of his food and the things he lives from? There is one flag that flies over these 48 States, and there is no law whereby any group of people can be mistreated because of their way of living.
Gold: Díí la’ dizdiin dóó bi’ąą tseehíí t’ááłá’í dah na’at’a’ígíí k’ad nihá dah siłtsoozígíí biyaagi bíla’ ’ashdla’ii hináá shį́į́ be’iina’ nilíinii la’ biniinaa doo ’atí doolnííłgóó bee haz’ą́ ’akon
Translation: Haash yiníł’į́įł da t’áá íiyisí ch’iyáán dóó bee iiná biniyé’ łahgo diné bich’į’ hadzidilchxoshígíí? Díí 48 State ałtso bikáa’ t’áá łá’ naat’áanii bich’ah dah naaznilí, dóó doo beehaz’ą́ t’áá íiyisí łahgo diné’é bee iiná biniyé’ bich’į’ hadzidilchxoshííł da.

English: There is no law to provide for the imprisonment of people just because they make their own living independently.
Gold: Siih hasinii biniinaa yah ’anihi’dii’nííł dooleełgi la’ ’ádin
Translation: Doo beehaz’áanii t’áá íiyisí da dine’é naaznilígíí t’áá hó’ájít’éego bee ’iináago biniinaa.

English: So how does it happen that we were told these things?
Gold: ’Áko lá ha’át’éego lá ’ánihi’di’níí lá

English: We returned from there, and they (the police) began hauling away more womenfolk and young men (to jail).
Gold: ’Áko ’éí díí ’áádę́ę́’ nániikai dóó tsíłkéí yę́ę sáanii yę́ę da ’adajiyeehgo baa nízhdiikai
Translation: ’Áádę́ę́’ nináda’iishjidgo, aadóó bóólis sáanii dóó tsíłkéí siih nízinii t’áá ’ajį́’ yida’oolnáh bóólis bighan góne’.

English: Some of these were injured by the cars.
Gold: Ła’ t’áá ’ákǫ́ǫ́ chidí ’atídaboolíiłgo ’aadę́ę́’ hoolzhiizh
Translation: Ła’ t’áá ’éí chidí bits’ą́ą́dóó daneesxíí’

English: Some became sick from these injuries and died.
Gold: Ła’ t’áá ’éí yits’ą́ą́dóó ka dadeeskaigo ’ádaadin daazlį́į́
Translation: Ła’ díí hoolzhiizhígíí biniinaa dájíghááh dóó ’ádajidin

English: In one case they were taking a woman to jail and she fell unconscious.
Gold: ’Éí ’éí siláago ła’ sáanii t’áá tádazhdiyeehgo doo bił ’ééhoozin da lá ’akon
Translation: T’ááłáádę́ę́’ asdzáán yę́ę da ’adajiyeehgo ’ánádįįh

English: This is a woman that we call Yellow hair, and who comes from White Rock Mesa.
Gold: ’Asdzą́ą́ Tsii’ łitsoii dabidii’ní Tsé Łigai Dah ’Azkánídóó
Translation: Díí asdzą́ą́ éí Tsiiʼ Łitso wolyé, dóó Tsé Łigaii Deezʼáhídi nilį́.

English: In view of the fact that she became unconscious they merely hauled her back home and left her,
Gold: Bíni’ ’ánádįįhgo ’áłt’ąą ńléí bighan yę́ędi ńdadzisgį́į́ lá
Translation: ’Áko doo bił ’ééhoozin da biniinaa t’áá íiyisí bighan náádiyeeh dóó hodeeł’į́.

English: instead of taking her on as they should have.
Gold: ’Áko t’áá ndajiyéhégi le’ ’ádadziidzaa
Translation: Doo bił dahaz’ą́ t’áá íiyisígíí da bik’ijį’.

English: Why should she be taken home after she fainted?
Gold: ’Éí diné doo bił ’ééhoozingóó shį́į́ ’áłt’ąą ha’át’íí biniiyé bighandi ndadzisgį́ ’akon
Translation: Ha’át’íísh ’ánádįįhgo bighan yę́ędi ’ádínídááh?

English: There were several cases of this kind.
Gold: ’Éí díkwíidi shį́į́ ’ákódzaa
Translation: Díí ’áhoot’éego daats’íí’ hólǫ́.

English: That is how we were abused.
Gold: ’Éí bee ts’ídá bidziilgo ’atí nihi’dool’įįd
Translation: ’Ákót’éego doo nihíł yá’át’ééh níłk’eh da ni’

English: All in all it was a sad story indeed.
Gold: ’Éidí doo hasht’é’égóó bąąh yíní ’akon
Translation: T’áá ałtso éí hane’ t’áá íiyisí doo yá’át’ééh da.

English: Many of our womenfolk died.
Gold: Nihizáanii daashį́į́ néelą́ą́’ ’ádin silį́į́’
Translation: Nihasáanii daashį́į́ neelą́ą́’ ’ádin silį́į́

English: Many of our men died.
Gold: Nihahastóí daashį́į́ neelą́ą́’ ’ádin silį́į́
Translation: Nihihastį́í daashį́į́ néelą́ą́’ ’ádin silį́į́’

English: Children died for lack of meat.
Gold: Kodóó ’áłchíní ’ach’ą́ dabíłtsééd
Translation: ’Áłchíní ’ach’ą́ ’ádaat’éii biníí’ ahool’ą́ą’.

English: When they were taken to the hospital they were immediately given soup
Gold: ’Éí bąą ’azee’ál’į́įdi yiltéehgo t’áá ’áko kodę́ę́’ ’atoo’ yikáał łeh
Translation: ’Azee’ál’į́ígóó ndahaasht’eezhgo jó k’ad t’áá jíík’ehgo át’óół yíiyá.

English: and milk.
Gold: ’Abe’ yikááł łeh ’akon
Translation: Dóó ’abe’

English: These were the only foods on which they could get well there.
Gold: Jó díí t’éiyá bee yá’át’ééh ninádahadleeh ’áadi ’akon
Translation: Díí t’áá íiyisí ch’iyáánígíí ’éídi bik’ehgo daná’azt’e’.

English: At the time when we could provide our own soup and milk the children were well.
Gold: Kodi ’atoo’ nihee hólǫ́ǫ́dą́ą́’ ’abe’ nihee hólǫ́ǫ́dą́ą́’ ’éí yá’át’ééh ńt’éé’ ’akon
Translation: ’Ákógíí t’áá nihí atsį́į́’ dóó béégashii bíjį́’ hólǫ́ǫgo, ’áłchíní yá’át’ééhgo danilį́į́’.

English: Some of the men with whom I made the trip to Washington were put in jail on that account.
Gold: ’Áko hastóí ńléí Wááshindoongóó bił nisiskai yę́ęni’ t’áá ’éí da biniinaa yah ’adajiiznil
Translation: Hastóí t’áá ałts’íísí Wááshindoongóó shikaadééł yę́ęni’ biniinaa yah ’abi’doo’nil

English: Every day I figured that they would come for me,
Gold: K’adę́ę ga’ yah ’ashi’dilt’e’ lá nááneiiniisdzįįh
Translation: T’áá’ákwíí shí ná’oolkiłgo shí náádeyááł,

English: but they didn't put me in jail.
Gold: ’Áko ndi shí ’éí t’áadoo yah ’adashidzist’e’ da
Translation: ’Éí ’éí doo shí ’awáalya biyi’ yishááh da

English: There was a man sitting here a while ago that I don't believe was taken to jail either.
Gold: Kǫ́ǫ́ hastiin ’aadę́ę́’ ła’ dah sidáa ni’ ’éí daats’í ’ałdó t’áadoo yah ’adajist’e’ da
Translation: Shádi’ááh díídi hastiin hólǫ́; shí doo nisin da jeiłgóó deeya dííkwii.

English: That is the way we were treated.A great number of the people's livestock was taken away.
Gold: ’Éí daashį́į́ néelą́ą́’ diné bilį́į́’ ’ádajisdįįd
Translation: Díí t’áá éígo nihá át’é. Diné bilį́į’ lání bináádoo’nil.

English: Although we were told that it was to restore the land, the fact remains that hunger stood with their mouths open to devour us,
Gold: Kéyah náhiidoo’naał ha’níi ndi kodę́ę́’ dichin nihiyah déezhch’a
Translation: Bikéyah náásdlį́į́’ binahjį’ nihaa ní’diilnishgo, nít’ę́ę́’ dichin nihiyááhígíí naaznil.

English: as well as poverty.
Gold: Łahdę́ę́’ té’é’į́ ’akon
Translation: Té’é’į́ yę́ę da

English: Before the stock that remained could reproduce, people slit the animals' throats to satisfy their starving children.
Gold: ’Éí ’akwe’íígi nihigha yii’nííł ’adoołchíłę́ęni’ ha’áłchíní dichin bi’niighą́ąhgo t’áá ’áko bizázhdígish
Translation: Tł’ízí dóó dibé hani’ígíí doo yiilá da shádi’nííłígíí, diné’é béésh bee bizis yisxishgo ’áłchíní ayóo deeshááłígíí bá ch’iyáán yina’á.

English: Before the sheep could bear young the children's shoes would wear out.
Gold: ’Adoołchíłę́ęni’ t’áá ’áko ha’áłchíní bikee’ ńdadit’o’
Translation: Dibé yázhí doo dahoodleeł da shį́į́’ígíí ’Áłchíní késhjéé’ yiyiiltsáʼ.

English: People would say, "Where can a sheep be sold?"
Gold: Haa’í yee’ dibé ndahaniih ha’niih
Translation: Diné yáníłti’, “Háadi dibé yíyááłígíí?”

English: When they heard of a place they would drive a couple of animals there.
Gold: T’áá ’áko ’ákǫ́ǫ́ ła’ jinooyoł łeh
Translation: Bikéyah baa ’ałháníłti’go naaki naaldlooshii ’aadę́ę́’ kóyaa yinaalnééh ńt’éé’

English: So instead of the stock increasing, it became less and less.
Gold: ’Áko háá’doolchíłę́ęni’ t’áá bi’ohgi bi’oh silį́į́’
Translation: Áko da’ádíníłígíí doo ’ałníí’go yáhoot’ééł da, t’áá ’alá’ígo ’alá’ígo áhoot’é.

English: And today one hears of many people who have come to possess stock permits for no reason at all (i.e. the permits are not filled or they have no more stock).
Gold: ’Éí k’ad t’áá ’ákónéehee k’ad naaltsoos bik’ehgo na’nilkaadí bee haz’aanii wolyéii t’áadoo biniiyéhégóó dah yiltsosii lą’í silį́į́’
Translation: Dííjį́’ t’áá ałtsoní dine’é t’áá íiyisí naaltsoos ’ałníí’ dah łichí’ígíí yíłnááhígíí nahalin (naaltsoos ’ałníí’ dah łichí’ígíí doo baa na’áłwo’ da, ’áádóó doo lį́į’ dahólóní da).

English: There is no stock with which to replace what is gone.
Gold: ’Áko t’áadoo bá ńdoolyééłdę́ę’ da ’akon
Translation: Nánináígíí bá náá’oolkił béégashii, dibé dóó tł’ízí doo hólǫ́ da.

English: It has come to the pass that there is not a place from which they can get a single sheep.
Gold: ’Éí t’áadoo dibé bá ńdooltééłdę́ę’ da silį́į́’
Translation: K’ad t’áá jíík’ehgo háádę́ę́’ t’áá íiyisí dibé doo hólǫ́ da.

English: Now there has come a lending program.
Gold: Jó ’akon k’ad béeso ’a’ii’nííł náádaha’ní ’akon
Translation: K’ad béeso bąąh dahwiihígíí bee naat’á hólǫ́.

English: It has as its purposes
Gold: ’Áko díí ga’ biniiyé lá ’azlį́į́’ ’akon
Translation: Biniiyégo bee hólǫ́

English: the restoration of the sheep,
Gold: Díí ga’ bee dibé ńdahodoodleeł lá ’akon
Translation: Dibé náádooleełígíí

English: the goats, the cattle and the horses.
Gold: Díí ga’ bee tł’ízí ńdeidoodzįįł lá béégashii łį́į́’ da
Translation: Tł’ízí, béégashii dóó łį́į’

English: But now I hear that only the people who have sheep, cattle and other things, or who are getting along well economically, will be given loans.
Gold: ’Áko ’éí ’éí k’ad nihich’į’ nináánát’i’go k’ad diists’a’go diné dibé bee hólóonii t’éiyá béégashii bee hólóonii t’éiyá t’áadoo le’é bee hólóonii yá’át’éehgo dah yigáałii díí t’éiyá béeso ba’doo’nił
Translation: Áko k’ad t’áá íiyisí dibé dóó béégashii dóó łáá’ áníí’í hołónígíí, dóó béeso bee hazhó’ógo ííná’ dahaz’ą́ągo danilį́į́’ diné, bee naalyééh dooleeł jini.

English: A person who has no sheep is refused a loan.
Gold: Kodóó t’áadoo le’é dibé da ’ádingo ’éí ni ’éí dooda
Translation: Dibé doo bí hólǫ́ daígíí Diné doo bee bąąh dah oolkił da

English: He is told that he has nothing with which to repay it.
Gold: Ni t’áadoo nináóódléłí da
Translation: ’Éí t’áadoo bee nááhályaa’dę́ę’ da hólǫ́ yá’áhoot’į́į́ł

English: So that is a new source of trouble for us.
Gold: Jo kót’éego nihich’į’ nikináádiit’i’
Translation: Áko díí ’éí nihá hóóchį’ bina’ígíí t’áá íiyisígíí.

English: It seems as though they tell them, "Go starve to death, you people who have nothing! You are taking up needed space."
Gold: ’Éí ’aají t’áá gééd yínáłígíí ’éí bíni’ dichin niiłhé niniinaa doo haz’ą́ą da hojiní nahalin
Translation: Ńt’ée’go baa yáníłti’, “Násdi’ dóó daazts’íídgo doo iiná da, doo hólǫ́ǫ́’ da íiyisí diné! Yá’át’éehígíí bikáa’ hadiidla’.”

English: There are no permits for the new generation of young men and women.
Gold: ’Índa tsíłkéí ch’ikéí da k’ad hanáánoot’áanii bibee haz’áanii ’ádin
Translation: Tsíłkéí dóó asdzání yázhí kééhat’íinii bich’į’ naaltsoos na’nilkaadí doo hólǫ́ da.

English: It would seem that they are merely headed for starvation.
Gold: ’Éí ’éí bíni’ dichin bidooghą́ą́ł jó kóne’ yilkił nahalin
Translation: Łahgo t’áá íiyisí dichin ndahałtseed.

English: When we went to the east we asked for schools and hospitals,
Gold: ’Áko díí k’ad ha’a’aahdi niikaidą́ą́’ ’azee’ál’į́ dadii’níi ni’ ’ólta’ dadii’níi ni’
Translation: Ha’a’aahgóó niikaigo ’ólta’ dóó ’azee’ál’į́’ nisin

English: but alas the school that we did have (here at Kayenta) was closed.
Gold: Yę́ęni’ kǫ́ǫ́ ’ólta’ ńt’éé’ ’akon nihits’ą́ą́’ ’ałch’į’ ’ánályaa
Translation: Nít’į́ ’áłahgo Kwe’é Tó Dínéeshzhee’di nihí ’ólta’ éí jííltsááh.

English: The hospital was closed.
Gold: ’Ázee’ál’į́į́ ńt’éé’ nihits’ą́ą́’ ’ałch’į’ ’ánályaa
Translation: ’Azee’ál’į́į’ ’ałch’į’ ’ánályaa

English: The latter has not been restored to the present day.
Gold: ’Éí dííjį́į́góó t’ah doo náhii’naah da
Translation: Łah ńt’éé’ éí doo náhásdlį́į́’ da.

English: There is still no hospital.
Gold: ’Azee’ál’ínę́ę t’ahdii ’ádin
Translation: Łahgo ’azee’ál’į́į́ doo hólǫ́ǫ́ da.

English: At present they come over to give us some encouragement, but that is all.
Gold: ’Áko k’ad t’óó bínihidi’nól’áahgo k’ad kǫ́ǫ́ yoołkááł
Translation: K’ad nihí baa t’áá ’ádíyídígo yá’át’ééh bizaad yáłti’ígíí shį́į́ kwii ní’áázh, ndi t’áá éíí ’akon

English: It must be an awfully long distance to Washington.
Gold: ’Áko ha’át’íí shį́į́ nízaad lá
Translation: T’áá shoodí Wááshindoongóó t’áá íiyisí ’áłk’idígíí nilį́.

English: First they have to send money across the sea to Europe to take care of things there.
Gold: Háadi shį́į́ tónteel yónaanídi ’áltsé hasht’e dahodoonííł ha’níigo ’áajigo ’áajigo ’éiyá béeso ’adahidit’aah
Translation: T’áá áádóó bee’eldǫ́ǫhtsoh tónteel yónaaníjí Éérop déé’ yídaalyaa, góne’ binaahaz’ą́ągo.

English: On the other hand, we're right here before their eyes,
Gold: Kǫ́ǫ́ hayaagóó shiijaa’ kǫ́ǫ́ nihiyaagóó shiijaa’ Wááshindoondi kééhoht’íinii
Translation: Ndi, díídi t’áá íiyisí binaaghaa’ danihá.

English: but some of you who are our national leaders must first appropriate money for the Germans and the Japanese because those people are said to be starving.
Gold: Nihinant’a’í danohłíinii kodóó ch’ééh nihída’dííiíikeedgo jó danihilááhgóó da Béésh Bich’ahí dichin bi’niighą́ Naats’ózí dichin bi’niighą́ ha’níigo ’áajigo ’áłtsé béeso ’adahidit’ah
Translation: Nídí, nihí Naahást’éí bikáa’gi naat’áanii nít’éé’ t’áá íiyisí, Béésh Bich’ahii Bikéyah bidine’é dóó Jóópan bidine’é bich’į’ béeso t’áá ałtsé hadilyeedooleeł, biniinaa díí dine’é dichin nitsaa yinízinígíí.

English: Those people made war upon you
Gold: ’Áko ’aadę́ę́’ nihitsiits’iin yiyííbaah
Translation: ’Éí diné níná’níłkaad

English: and wanted to kill you, but you say that they must come first; that they must eat first.
Gold: ’Aadę́ę́’ ts’ídá tsį́įłgo ndiyoolyééł ts’ídá ’áajį’ t’éiyá ’éí t’éiyá yee ndiilkaal yę́ę k’ad ’éí ’áajį’ ’i’doołnah diní ’akon
Translation: Béésh Bich’ahí dóó Naats’ózí nihídii’ náhást’į́į́’ nízin, ńléí ’áajigo ’áłtsé hóshááł; ’áajigo ’áłtsé ’i’idoołnah dadohní ’akon

English: In the east they are saying that they are becoming aware, that’s why it is like that.
Gold: Jó díí k’ad ha’a’aahdi dahwiilyąąh ha’níigo ’áko ’éí bąą k’ad ’ákót’é ’akon
Translation: Ha’a’aahdi náá bééhózin dajiníigo, biniinaa éí t’áá ’íiyisí ’at’é.

English: We were here on our own land a long time before you white people came, increasing rapidly, but you came and reduced us to poverty.
Gold: ’Áko kodę́ę́’ t’áá shiidą́ą’dii nihiyaadę́ę́’ shiijaa’ yę́ę ’índa t’áá shiidą́ą’dii nihikéyah tsį́į́ł niit’į́įłgo nihaa hisoohkai yę́ę k’ad kǫ́ǫ́ dichin biih danihisoonil
Translation: Hááláá’ nihikéyahdi danilį́į́’ nihí; bilagáana doo ałníí’ daígíí, t’áá ałts’áádgo shíígo daniilyaa; ’áko bilagáana ałníí’go, nihí kǫ́ǫ́ té’é’į́ biih danihisoonil.

English: You have reduced us to poverty, but you pass us over, saying that the Germans must eat.
Gold: Kǫ́ǫ́ té’é’į́ biih danihisoonilgo nihilááhgóó ńléí háadi shį́į́ Béésh Bich’ahí ’i’idoołnah dadohní ’akon
Translation: Kǫ́ǫ́ dichin biih danihisoonil, ’áko nihá adit’ą́ą́’, Béésh Bich’ahí ’i’doołnah diní ’akon.

English: So, my leaders who live in Washington, give us back something that is worthwhile.
Gold: ’Áko díí k’ad kǫ́ǫ́ kééhat’ínígíí kǫ́ǫ́ kééhwiit’ínígíí ’áko t’áá shǫǫdí t’áá doozhǫǫgo ha’át’íi da bee nihąąh tsínídóhkees shinant’a’í Wááshindoondi kéédahoht’íinii
Translation: ’Áko Wááshindoondi daniilį́ shinaat’áanii, łikanígíí ná nihá hólǫ́ dooleeł.

English: I do not speak thus to be critical of you.
Gold: Doo nihitaa ’ash’į’go ’ánihidishníi da
Translation: Doo nihí bá naniséego ’ánihidishníi da

English: I do not speak thus out of hate for you.
Gold: Doo nihijooshłáago ’ánihidishníi da
Translation: Doo nihibá doo ayóó nihíłnííh da biniinaa ’ánihidishníi da

English: It is my plea.
Gold: Nánihooshkąągo ’ánihidishní
Translation: Shisódizin ’át’é

English: I say it because all of my neighbors feel likewise.
Gold: Díí k’ad diné bił kééhasht’íinii t’áá ’ałtso ’ákwíinízingo ’ádíshní
Translation: T’áá ’ałtso nahgóó shik’éí danilíinii díkwíí danízin biniinaa ’ádíshní

English: All of my neighbors say so.
Gold: T’áá ’ałtso ’ákóníigo ’ádíshní ’akon
Translation: Diné bił kééhasht’íinii t’áá ’áłtso éí daníłnii’.

English: When I had a husband and a lot of sheep I was happy.
Gold: Diné shee hólǫ́ǫdą́ą́’ yá’át’éehgo naasháá ńt’éé’ ’índa shilį́į’ da dahólǫ́ǫgo
Translation: Hastiinę́ę dóó dibé ałts’óózígíí shíł hólǫ́go shí éí hózhǫ́.

English: Then when it came my sheeps' turn to be acted upon, they were all driven away from me.
Gold: ’Áádóó shilį́’ę́ę bee shaa hwiiníst’įįdgo t’áá naakai ńt’éé’ t’óó sits’ą́ą́’ yah ’anoolkaad
Translation: T’áá áko shidibé bá ánííłnii’go, t’áá íiyisí shí yiiláh.

English: They were driven into a corral and I was told to select the ones that were the best.
Gold: T’áá nił yá’ádaat’éhígíí t’éiyá ch’ééní’nííł shi’doo’niid
Translation: Gáshjaaʼ biyiʼ doołkááhgo tʼáá yáʼátʼéehígíí yíshléí shí yíníłtiʼ

English: That hurt me and I just bowed my head.
Gold: ’Aadóó t’óó bik’ee yaa dínésht’ą́
Translation: ’Áko shijááh dóó t’áá shitsii’ yídeelyá.

English: I just sent my children over and they selected some.
Gold: ’Áłchíní t’éiyá ’ákǫ́ǫ́ ’eekaigo ła’ ch’ídayiiznil
Translation: Shí t’áá k’ad ’áádę́ę́’ ’áłchíní yídiiltį́ dóó łá’ yíníłnii’.

English: We became despondent over it.
Gold: Jó ’aadóó bik’ee ka deekai
Translation: Bik’ee danáádésdzá

English: My husband became sick from worry,
Gold: Hastiin bił naash’aash ńt’éé’ yik’ee ka deeyá ’akon
Translation: Hastiinę́ę nitsáhákees biniinaa bąąh dahoo’a’

English: and these officials went about in their cars even at night.
Gold: ’Áko tł’ée’ ndi t’áá ’áko kodę́ę́’ ła’ chidí hoł yilwoł łeh
Translation: ’Aadóó díí beehaz’áanii dine’é tł’ée’go t’áá íiyisí chidí bił yah anááh.

English: Early in the morning one would be going about.
Gold: Hool’įįhgo da t’áá ’áko ła’ yilwo’
Translation: T’óó haiłkááhdą́ą́’ na’níyá jiní

English: They even interrupted our sleep.
Gold: ’Áko ’éí ’ákót’éego hazhó’ó da’iilwosh yę́ę nihibił dajiiníísh
Translation: T’áá íiyisí nihí náálʼą́ yinaaznil.

English: They did this on account of our sheep and our way of life.
Gold: T’áá nihí nihilį́’ígíí dóó t’áá nihí nihina’nitinígíí biniinaa
Translation: Nihí dibé dóó nihí bee iiná biniinaa ’ádaat’į́

English: When we drove our sheep to the dipping vat some more were taken away.
Gold: Táada’agisgóó ninááda’neelkaadgo ’áadi ła’ nihits’ą́ą́’ bináádoo’nil
Translation: Dibé nihí bąąh na’álkááhígíí góó daashjaałgo, ts’ídá áłgo nihá yah ’anoolkaad.

English: It was there that my husband said,"You people are indeed heartless.
Gold: ’Áadi ’índa hastiinę́ę ’ájíní Doo lá dó’ yówéé’ ’ádanoht’ée da lá
Translation: ’Áájį’ shihastiin yíníł’į́, "T’áá íiyisí doo iits’į́ nihí hólǫ́ da."

English: You have now killed me.
Gold: K’ad lá ’índa dasisoołhį́ ni
Translation: K’ad shínídii’ní

Gold: Shigaan k’ídasoołne’
Translation: Shilá’ k’ídasoołne’

English: You have cut off my legs.
Gold: Shijáád k’ídasoołne’
Translation: Shijáád k’ídasoołne’

English: You have taken my head off.
Gold: Sitsiits’iin nda’doo’ą́
Translation: Shitsii’ k’ídasoołne’

Gold: Ha’át’íísh dó’ bee bighą́ą́h ńdeeshdááł jó shinahat’a’ dahisoołne’
Translation: Shí baa doo ha’át’íí’ hólǫ́ da.

English: This is the end of the trail, he said.
Gold: K’ad lá nihonít’i’ ni jidííniid ’akon
Translation: Díí ’adeetiin be’ak’a’ígíí ’át’é ní jiní

English: This happened, and it wasn't long before my husband fell ill.
Gold: ’Éí ’ákódzaa dóó t’áadoo ts’ídá náhodíníilzhíshí hastiinę́ę bąąh dahoo’a’
Translation: ’Éí ’áadi ’ákódzaa dóó dah neezdáá t’áadoo ndi kojí diné yá’áhoot’į́.

English: It was no doubt the worry that sickened him.
Gold: Bik’ee shą’ bíní yii’a’go t’áá ’éí bits’ą́ą́dóó bąąh dahoo’a’
Translation: Nízingo bihodíílnih biniiyé ádziih.

English: He was sick all winter, and at the beginning of spring he died.
Gold: Haigo hąąh  dah hoo’a’go ńléí dąąjį’ ch’ééhoolzhiizhgo ’áajį’ nizhniníłna’
Translation: Haigo t’áá ałtso doo bił hózhó da, dóó dá’ák’ehjígo áłtségo deest’į́.

English: These two events, the loss of my sheep and the loss of my husband, made me feel terribly unhappy.
Gold: Dibé bee hinishnáanii sits’ą́ą́’ ’anoolkaad dóó kojí diné sits’ą́ą́’ ’ádinígíí biniinaa naaki ’ahąąh baa yínígo déyá
Translation: Díí naaki ánííłníí’, shidibé doo shihólǫ́ǫ́ da dóó shí hastiin doo shihólǫ́ǫ́ da, áko ayóó shí éí díkwíí’.

English: I was despondent,
Gold: T’áá ’éí bik’ee ka náádésdzá
Translation: Jó shí yínígo nishłį́

English: and I am still so today.

English: I had five sons then,
Gold: Sha’áłchíní ’éí diné ’ashdla’ ’íídą́ą́’

English: We were all dependent on the small amount of stock granted to us on the permit (lit. we all climbed onto this tiny permit.)
Gold: Kót’éego naaltsoos ’ałníí’ dah łichí’ígíí t’įįhdígo bikáa’go bikáá’ niniikai
Translation: T’áá ałtso díí naaltsoos bik’ehgo na’azłání ’áłts’óó’ bina’áł’ą́.

English: We could not always make ends meet (lit. some of us would fall off it and would grab about for something to reestablish our balance and get us back onto it.)
Gold: Bidah ’anídadiiltałgo ’áádę́ę́’ dadiijihgo háádahii’nééh
Translation: Doo t’ááłá’ígo nihí t’áá ajiłii da; adáádį́į́’ danida’ahiilziłgo, háádida haa ’ohniidiiłnihgo nihit’ááł hozhoogo ályaa, nihí bidah náázhdítł’į́į́’.

English: In the course of getting one back onto it, another would fall off, so we really had to work closely together in order to stay on this permit.
Gold: Náánáłahjí ła’ bidah náázhdítłishgo kojį’ ńda’ahiilził nahalingo hááda’ahiyiidzį́įsgo k’ad kwe’é kóníłtsogo dah łichí’ígi t’éiyá bik’i dah naháatą́ nahalin
Translation: T’áá łá’ bikáa’ náádii’nííłgo la’ dadiijih, dóó naaltsoos ’ałníí’ bikáa’ doo dadiijih da biniinaa t’áá ákót’éego ałch’į’ bee nidaníł’į́.

English: We suffered from everything, from hunger, from lack of meat and from despondency.
Gold: T’áá ’ałtsoní bik’ee ti’dahwii’nį́įhgo dichin ’ádaat’éii ’índa ’ach’ą́ ’ádaat’éii ’índa yíní ’ádaat’éii da t’áá ’ałtso
Translation: T’áá ałtso nihidiits’ą́, ts’íídá biniiyé, bitsį’ doo hólǫ́ da biniiyé, dóó hodíníiłígíí biniiyé.

English: The Special Grazing Regulation is like a killing disease from which one cannot sleep.
Gold: Naałniih ńda’digą́ąhii biniinaa doo da’awoshígíí nahalinii ’át’éé lá díí naaltsoos ’ałníí’ dah łichíí’ há’nínígíí
Translation: Díí Diné bá yádaałti’ii t’áá ’áhoot’éego ts’ídá ’áńt’į́į́’, dóó tł’óółgo doo si’ą́ą́’ da

English: We cannot live because of it.

Translation: Biniinaa doo nihilį́ da.

English: One will not walk pleasantly.

English: I was just a little bit scared.

Translation: T’áá bíyó shił boosh’ááh ńt’éé’

Gold: Kót’éego shidine’é bikéyah bikáá’góó táhodííle’
Translation: Áko díí éí shí hane’ shidine’é bikéyah bikáa’diígíí.

English: I looked the place over from there.
Gold: Dóó ’áádę́ę́’ ha’íísid
Translation: ’Áádę́ę́’di kéyah yishtsááh

English: And it is true.
Gold: ’Áko t’áá ’aaníí ’át’éé lá
Translation: Áádóó ’éí ’aaníí

English: In some places cattle and horses were just standing about, probably on account of the crusted snow.
Gold: Łahgóó béégashii ’índa łį́į’ da t’óó naazį́ yas danitł’izígíí shį́į́ biniinaa
Translation: Łahgóó béégashii dóó łį́į́’ t’óó naazį́, yas tł’eesgo biniinaa shį́į́.

English: They would break through this crust, and just stand there.
Gold: Yikáá’ hahakáahgo yiníká dahatłííshgóó ’ákǫ́ǫ́ t’óó naazį́
Translation: Díí yás danitł’izígíí yideezláago, t’óó naazį́.

English: They wouldn't go on.
Gold: Doo náás dadikáah da
Translation: Doo t’áá íiyisí náá deyá da

English: Then they would starve or freeze to death right where they stood.
Gold: ’Áko t’áá ’áajį’ dichin ndahałtseed dóó ndajiidlóóh
Translation: ’Áko t’áá ałtsonígi dichin biniinaa daajį́’ łeh doodago atsiniltł’ish biniinaa daajį́’ łeh

English: In some places the sheep were kept in the corrals all day long.
Gold: ’Índa łahgóó dibé bighan biyi’góó dibé t’áá naazhjée’go ’ada’ii’aah lá
Translation: Łahgóó abínígo t’áá jíík’ehgo dibé k’ááhígíí iildááh.

English: People would merely bring them branches.
Gold: ’Áko ’éí t’óó ’ił bił yah ’adajiishood
Translation: Diné t’áá t’óó bich’į’ tsin yázhí na’aldleeł łeh ńt’éé’.

English: This is how my people suffered.
Gold: Kót’éego shidine’é ’atíbi’diilyaa lá
Translation: Jó ’akon ’ákót’éego shidine’é ’atíbi’diilyaa

English: This was my people's disaster.
Gold: Kót’éego shidine’é bide ’áhoot’éé lá
Translation: ’Éí shidine’é baa nitsaa doo yá’át’ééh da áhoot’éí át’é.

English: Many people lost stock.
Gold: Diné bilį́į́’ t’óó ’ahayóí bits’ą́ą́’ bináádíníídee’ lá
Translation: Diné t’óó ’ahayóí dibé dóó béégashii dah nahalį́į́’.

English: Maybe the range riders and district supervisors feel thankful for it because it reduced the stock
Gold: Łį́į́’ neilózí ’índa naat’áaniishchíín danilíinii dibé bi’oh ’áńdoolnííł daanínę́ęni’ ’éí shį́į́ t’áá hazhó’ó bił da’ahéhee’
Translation: Dííshjéé’, béégashii bikéyahdi na’ałkaahii dóó naaznilígíí naal’į́į́’í díí biniinaa ahéhee’ yínízin, t’áá ’áko béégashii dóó dibé naazhnííł.

English: This is no small matter.
Gold: Doo níłt’éegiísh ’ánihi’diilyaa
Translation: Díí doo t’áá íiyisí át’é da.

English: God punished us.
Gold: God wolyéii ’atínihiilaa
Translation: God ’atínihi’diilyaa

English: That’s what I think.
Gold: Shí nisingo baa ntséskees
Translation: ’Éí shí nisin.

English: There is a passage where God says that the people will be punished, and that's what happened.
Gold: Háadi shį́į́ God ’ání ’atínihidi’doolnííł nihíłnínę́ęni’ ’éí k’ad ’ákónihi’diilyaa
Translation: Diyin yáłti’ígíí t’áá íiyisí éí diné bee naalyeeh dooleeł jiní, dóó áko éí ajiłkee’.

Gold: K’ad tseebííts’áadah nááhaiídą́ą́’ ’ałdó’ ’ákódzaa ni’

Translation: ’Íídą́ą́ ’éí nihí baa ’áníłti’

Gold: Kót’éego ’át’é
